<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Impromptus&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Impromptus</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Fantasias&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Fantasias</a></span>;
